#### Dagger

Any forearm length blade can be called a dagger, and there are as many designs as there are cultures in existence. The master can make lightning fast attacks even while they
focus their attention elsewhere.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Light, Thrown (20/60) |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Light, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master Ability | As an ability action, you can make an off-hand attack if you haven't used it for an attack or held your action for an attack. |

#### Estoc

Any forearm length blade can be called a dagger, and there are as many designs as there are cultures in existence. The master can make lightning fast attacks even while they
focus their attention elsewhere.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Brace |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Penetrate, Puncture |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Keen, Lunge, Penetrate, Puncture |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Keen, Lunge, Penetrate, Puncture |
| Master Ability | As an ability action, you can make an attack with this weapon if you haven't held your action for an attack. |

\column

#### Kukri

A thick, hooked blade with a cutting edge on the inside, performing more like a handaxe than a dagger. The wing shape flies somewhat like a boomerang, and the master uses its forward curve to hamstring enemies.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Thrown (40/80) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Keen, Thrown (40/80) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Keen, Thrown (40/120), Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Disarm, Keen, Thrown (40/120), Trip |
| Master Ability | When you hit with a trip attack, your target's speed is reduced by 10ft. It may attempt a Constitution check at the end of its turn, ending the effect on success. |

#### Rapier

A thin, tapered sword with a wide guard and extra weight in the handle for maximum control with the tip, prized as the pinnacle of finesse. Rapier masters are unmatched duelists with perfect reach and riposte.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Puncture |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Puncture |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Lunge, Puncture |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Lunge, Puncture |
| Master Ability | If you are wielding only a rapier, you can add d4 to your damage rolls. If you are dual wielding a light weapon, instead add +1 to weapon AC. |

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Dueling Blades }}

\page

#### Saber

Slightly curved, single-edged, one-handed weapons often with a basket hilt, allowing expert deflections off the curve. The master's defensive capabilities with the saber are unmatched among dueling blades.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Deflect |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Keen |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Keen, Light |
| Master Ability | If you are wielding a single saber, you may add d4 to your deflect rolls. While wielding two sabers, if you reduce an enemy's damage to 0, you gain the use of your reaction back. |

#### Sai

A dagger sized weapon made famous in Okinawa, consisting of a sharpened metal rod with two forward swept prongs as a guard, making it easy to block and trap enemy weapons. The master parries and disarms in an instant with the prongs.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Nimble |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Conceal, Nimble |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Conceal, Disarm, Nimble |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Conceal, Deflect, Disarm, Nimble |
| Master Ability | You gain +1 weapon AC. If an enemy misses you with a melee attack, as a reaction you can force them to succeed on a saving throw or drop the weapon. |

#### Shortsword

Swords between 2ft-3ft in length with as many different designs as there are cultures. Their wide and varied designs mean that a master can find the perfect form for their style.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Light |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Light |
| Master Ability | The balanced property applies to attachers. If you have advantage, you can roll damage and attachers twice and use the better result. |

\column

#### Sickle

A crescent-shaped blade derived from a farming tool with the cutting edge on the inside. A master with the sickle has learned to grab and hamstring with the reaping curve.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Keen |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Keen, Puncture |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Keen, Puncture, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Light, Keen, Puncture, Trip |
| Master Ability | When you hit with an entangle or trip attack, you deal full weapon damage and your enemy suffers -10ft to its speed until it succeeds on a Constitution check at the end of its turn. |

#### Smallsword

A needle-like blade with a narrow profile and a fine tip for fitting between plates of armor, often given a dome shaped guard to protect the hands while thrusting. The master has such control and poise that any distraction or detriment can be ignored with enough focus on the target.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Lunge, Penetrate |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Lunge, Penetrate |
| Master Ability | If you have advantage on your attack, you may add a d4 to your attack roll. If you have disadvantage on your attack, as an ability action, you may roll your choice of athletics or acrobatics check to negate the disadvantage. The DC is equal to your target's AC. |

#### Sword Breaker

A short weapon with notches on its spine, designed to catch, disarm, and in extreme cases, break the enemy's weapon. The master can disarm in an instant, and with another weapon, possibly break the enemy's sword.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Light |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Disarm, Light |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Disarm, Light |
| Master Ability | When you deflect, you can also force your enemy to succeed on your choice of an Athletics or Reflex Saving Throw or be disarmed. If your disarm attack is a critical hit, your enemy's mundane weapon is broken and unusable. |

#### Double Flail

Two flail heads, each with a separate chain attached to a single handle, whether they are attached at opposing ends, or attached at the same end. The Double flail is a difficult weapon to use effectively, and only the master really gets use out of individual heads, turning a potential miss into a new opportunity.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Trip, Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Trip, Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Trip, Versatile |
| Master Ability | When you suffer disadvantage but one dice would have hit, you deal 1 of the weapon's damage dice plus half of your weapon ability modifier, even though this still counts as a miss. If you have advantage and both dice hit, add your weapon ability modifier twice to the damage total. |

#### Light Flail

The familiar 2lb spiked ball at the end of a length of chain, attached to a short iron or wooden haft usually similar in length to a handaxe. The light flail sees lightning fast attacks turned into a great boon for the master, carrying the weapons speed and momentum into another attack if they miss.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Trip |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Light, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Light, Trip |
| Master Ability | You may reroll any attack you miss, but must take the new result. |

\column

#### Heavy Flail

A large spiked metal bar attached to a long handle, allowing one or two handed usage. The massive head and lengthy chain put it in the same sphere of war as the warhammer and battle axe. A master's binding and tripping attacks still harm their target if the enemy resists the maneuver.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Reach, Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Reach, Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Reach, Trip, Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Knockback, Penetrate, Reach, Trip, Versatile |
| Master Ability | If your target successfully saves against your weapon DC, you can make an attack as part of the same action. |

#### Pole Flail

A pole weapon with a spiked bar of the heavy flail at the end of a chain. The master learns to bind and wrap opponents, disrupting their footwork to allow their own free movement.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Heavy, Reach |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Knockback, Heavy, Reach |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Knockback, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Knockback, Penetrate, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | When you make a melee attack against a creature, you don't provoke opportunity attacks from that creature for the rest of the turn. |

\page

#### Meteor Hammer

A small weight attached to a rope or chain, used like a rope dart to make circular and explosive lunging attacks. A master can twirl the weapon around them with varying angles to strike any foe who might get near.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Conceal |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Conceal, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Conceal, Entangle, Lunge, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Conceal, Entangle, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Conceal, Disarm, Entangle, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | As a reaction you can enter a readied stance. Until the start of your next turn, you may make an attack against any creature that enters your reach, and doing so does not use your reaction. |

#### Nunchaku

The nunchaku is two rods bound by a rope or chain. By whipping around the body, a master can make lightning fast attacks to wield it like a Double Ended weapon.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Conceal |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Conceal, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Conceal, Light, Trip |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Conceal, Light, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Double Ended, Entangle, Conceal, Light, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | You can use the Double Ended property one handed. Dual wielding two nunchaku, you can attack twice with Double Ended. |

#### Trisectional Staff

A quarterstaff cut into three sections, each connected with a small length of chain or rope. A master uses this weapon's double hinges to strike in unpredictable ways, tripping or entangling with either end of the weapon.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Entangle, Trip |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Balanced, Double Ended, Entangle, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Balanced, Disarm, Double Ended, Entangle, Trip |
| Master Ability | Your Disarm, Entangle, and Trip attacks deal bludgeoning damage equal to your 1.5 times your weapon ability modifier. |

\column

#### Whip

The whip is treated as a melee weapon with 15ft reach. You can use a whip to grasp unattended small objects, or any reasonable handhold within range and if possible, you can pull the object to you. A whip master treats their whips as extensions of their hands.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Reach |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Reach, Trip |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Entangle, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Entangle, Keen, Light, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | When you disarm any creature, you choose to place the item anywhere in your reach, or use your reaction to catch it. An item in your reach that can be grabbed with the whip can be placed anywhere else in your reach. |

#### Whip Sword

A whip sword can be either a sword or a bladed whip. As an ability action, you change between the forms of your weapon. As a sword, it is similar to a longsword. As a whip, it gains reach, utility, and a target entangled by you takes your weapon's damage. A master can quickly change between forms as needed to attack enemies near their entangled prey.

| | Sword Form |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Lunge, Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Lunge, Puncture, Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Lunge, Puncture, Versatile |
| Master Ability | You may change between weapon forms freely. Additionally, when you hit with this weapon, you can choose to deal only your weapon ability modifier in damage and automatically entangle your enemy by changing to its whip profile. |

| | Whip Form |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Entangle, Reach |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Entangle, Reach, Trip |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Entangle, Keen, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Entangle, Keen, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | While an enemy is entangled, you can still attack it or any target within 5ft of it. |

#### Light Hammer

A short-handled hammer about the size of a handaxe and just as balanced for throwing. While a mace may shred armor, a hammer delivers precise blows that weaken the enemy, and a master can disorient the opponent for follow up attacks.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Thrown (10/40) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (10/40) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60) |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master Ability | When you score a critical hit, the enemy suffers a d6 penalty to their next check of any ability. |

#### Light Pick

A long, thin pick, mounted to a short haft, capable of precise, targeted piercing attacks that punch through armor with ease. Though not as stout as a war pick, the light pick allows more agile maneuvers, as well as balanced throwing. A master looks for the perfect opening, placing the pick into soft targets or between plates where armor is lacking.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Thrown (20/60) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (20/60), Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (20/60), Trip |
| Master Ability | Your Penetrate property ignores 3/4 of your target's armor bonus to their Armor Class. |

\column

#### Lucerne

A pole mounted, pronged hammer head for crushing blows on one side and a vicious hooking spike head for piercing and peeling armor on the other. The long haft allows the wielder to put devastating force behind the blows of this weapon. Lucerne masters swing at angles which force their enemies to choose between sacrificing equipment or flesh.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Penetrate, Puncture, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Penetrate, Puncture, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Penetrate, Puncture, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | If your enemy succeeds on the save from your Trip attack, they instead take normal weapon damage. |

#### Maul

A massive weapon near the size of a greataxe with an immensely weighted head, the maul can send foes staggering from even attempting to block such a massive weapon. Mauls always gain advantage when rolling an attack to destroy an object. The master finds the best ways to bully their opponents with the weight of this massive weapon.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Penetrate |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Penetrate, Trip |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Knockback, Penetrate, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Knockback, Penetrate, Trip |
| Master Ability | Your knockbacks move a target 10ft in a direction of your choosing. Creatures one size category larger than you do not gain advantage on the save, and you may attempt to knockback creatures two size categories larger, though they gain advantage on the save. Creatures three size categories larger than you are immune as usual. |

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Hammers and Picks }}

\page

#### Stiletto

A thin, round spike with a thin point and round cross section make it perfect for fitting between or outright puncturing through metal plates or rings. A master employs a host of grappling techniques as follow ups to their initial attacks.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Puncture, Light |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture, Light |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Conceal, Penetrate, Puncture, Light |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Conceal, Entangle, Penetrate, Puncture, Light |
| Master Ability | When your enemy is entangled, you can use your ability action to attempt a shove. |

#### Wall Pick

Similar in size to the light pick, with a longer, hooked spike to aid in climbing. In combat, the hook is used to grapple or disarm enemies while still able to puncture and pierce armor. A wall pick gives you advantage on climb checks and you can climb onto creatures any size category bigger than you. The master can grapple a foe as easily as they latch onto a wall.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Entangle, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Entangle, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60), Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Disarm, Entangle, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60), Trip |
| Master Ability | If your entangle attack misses, you can reroll the attack once but must take the new roll. If you roll a critical hit, your enemy is restrained and grappled. |

\column

#### War Hammer

Historically a lightweight, long-handled weapon around 3ft-4ft in length, designed to damage armored enemies. The small, pronged hammer head is often backed with a military pick or different style of face. A master of the warhammer carries momentum into each attack to send foes reeling.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Versatile |
| Master Ability | If you move at least 10ft in a straight line before your attack, your attack ignores an additional 1 AC if wielding it one handed, or 2 AC if two handing your war hammer. On a critical hit, your weapon damages the target's armor, permanently decreasing the armor class until the armor is repaired |

#### War Pick

A weaponized miner's pick, famously invented by militant mountain dwarves, refined worldwide for use against armored infantries. The pick comes in many forms but is usually a battle axe sized weapon with a reinforced spike on one end, and a narrow hammer opposite the spike. The master can strike vital areas, puncturing deeply to bleed the target out over time.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Puncture |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture, Trip |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture, Trip |
| Master Ability | If you score a critical hit your enemy begins to bleed. Roll a d10. At the start of its turn, the target takes this value as piercing damage, and takes 1 less each subsequent turn until 0 piercing damage. This damage stops if they receive any healing, or they spend an action to staunch the bleeding. If a target is affected by this bleeding damage, an additional critical hit will increase the bleed damage by your roll of a d10. It is up to your DM if your target is capable of bleeding. |

{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Hammers and Picks }}

### Polearms

#### Bladed Staff

A 6' staff weapon with a sword on each end, usually straight, but curved varieties exist. A bladed staff can be used to great effect, creating space around the wielder in a skirmish, or used as an effective spear with a wicked butt end. The master is able to attack as quickly with two blades as others are with only one, in lightning rapid fire strikes that take full advantage of the weapon's reach.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Balanced, Double Ended, Reach |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Balanced, Double Ended, Reach |
| Master Ability | When you use the double ended property, you do not need to be within 5ft of your target. |

#### Glaive

Perhaps the simplest of the polearms, a glaive is a short sword blade mounted on a long pole, used like a spear or a greatsword, the wide, sweeping slashes become useful for dealing with enemies much bigger than the wielder. While originally designed to be used by infantry against cavalry, in the hands of a master, a glaive is quite effective as a giant killer.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach |
| Master Ability | Against creatures of category size Large and larger, your damage is 3d6 instead of 2d6 |

\column

#### Guisarme

A sharpened and sturdy pruning hook, developed as a peasant weapon from modifying a farm tool. The curved hook of the blade allows the guisarme to be used as a tripping weapon or to pull foes from the saddle. A guisarme is a favorite of common militias who will face cavalry in battle, as the master can pull a knight from the saddle with relative ease.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Keen, Trip |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Keen, Trip |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Entangle, Heavy, Keen, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Barbed, Brace, Entangle, Heavy, Keen, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | Your trip attacks impose disadvantage to saving throws made to resist them and if you succeed against a mounted enemy, it is automatically pulled from its mount to prone |

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Polearms }}

\page

#### Lajatang

A rare and unusual double ended weapon, consisting of a 3-5ft shaft and a crescent blade fitted at each end, with the points of the crescents pointing away from the haft of the weapon, giving it essentially 2 outward facing spear points on each end. Lajatang masters are extremely rare, but are a whirling dervish of crescent blades and points, dangerous from all sides.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Heavy |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Heavy, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Double Ended, Heavy, Reach |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Double Ended, Heavy, Reach |
| Master Ability | On your turn, you can spend your reaction to enter a Defensive Stance, negating any flanking bonus or ability any enemy might have for flanking you or having the enemy's ally near you, such as pack tactics or sneak attack. You may use Double Ended twice on your turn, but your second attack must be against a different target than your first. |

#### Partisan

Much like a Glaive design, this pole weapon is essentially a shortsword blade mounted to a long haft, but keeps a wide cross guard at the base of the blade, trading sweeping cuts for defensive guards. The master Partisan uses the guard of their weapon like a shield at distance, and can even use it to protect allies.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach |
| Master Ability | You have +1 weapon AC. When an enemy lands an attack on an ally within your range, you may use your reaction to force the enemy to reroll the attack. |

\column

#### War Scythe

Whether mounted horizontally like a traditional farming implement, or mounted vertically like a glaive, a war scythe has its roots in a peasant militia looking to arm itself in times of war. A scythe in the right hands can be useful in combat, though it takes a practiced master to be truly effective. The master uses the scythe's reaping motion to deal horrible slashing wounds to the foes they trip in combat.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Keen, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Heavy, Keen, Puncture, Reach, Trip |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Keen, Puncture, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Entangle, Heavy, Keen, Puncture, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | Your trip attacks deal full weapon damage, and if you knock a creature prone, its speed is reduced by half. At the end of its turn, the enemy can attempt a Constitution check, ending the effect on a success. |

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Polearms }}

| Winged Spear | Piercing | d6 | d6 (d8) | d6 (d8) | d6 (d8) | d8 (d10) | 2 | 25 |

#### Godendag

A short spear with a heavy ball socket to hold the spear point, making use of sweeping bludgeons and weighted piercing attacks. The master makes full use of the added weight for powerful blows that set their enemy off balance.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Thrown (20/60) |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120), Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Disarm, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120), Trip |
| Master Ability | If you score a critical hit, the next attack against this target gains advantage. |

#### Harpoon

A barbed throwing spear with a welded ring, attached to a length of rope or chain so the target or harpoon can be retrieved. This weapon comes with 50ft of silk rope, which is reflected in the cost and weight. A master of the harpoon impales with ease and can swiftly reel in a harpooned prey.
:
On a hit, your enemy must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or be impaled, while a critical hit always impales.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Thrown (20/60) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Puncture, Thrown (20/60) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120) |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Barbed, Light, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120) |
| Master Ability | You drag an enemy toward you up to 20 feet, and your target suffers disadvantage to Strength while while it is impaled. |

#### Javelin

A light throwing spear balanced for flight but sturdy enough as a simple spear. A master can make an Olympian throw, puncturing shields so deeply, the enemy must pry the remnants out before it can be of any use in combat.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward, Light |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Light, Thrown (30/120) |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (30/120) |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (60/240) |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Light, Penetrate, Thrown (60/240) |
| Master Ability | When you score a critical, the target suffers a -2 AC penalty. On its turn an enemy can use an action to succeed on an Athletics check to pry the javelin free, destroying it in the process. |

#### Lance

Designed to unseat mounted enemies from the saddle, while on foot a lance imposes disadvantage against targets within 5ft, but while mounted gains One Handed and Penetrate. Masters leverage their mount's strength, allowing for devastating blows that knock enemies to the ground.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Reach |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Brace, Reach |
| Master Ability | You may attempt a Shove as an ability action. While mounted, after you successfully hit a target, you can attempt a shove as part of the same attack and gain advantage in the roll. Additionally, you no longer suffer disadvantage to attack rolls when you use this weapon on foot. |

{{pageNumber,auto}}
{{footnote Chapter VI: Equipment | Spears }}

\page

#### Pike

An 8-12 ft polearm designed for soldiers in a phalanx against an opposing line. A master with the pike fights as a phalanx soldier, striking so deftly they can stop a charging foe.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Penetrate, Reach |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Penetrate, Reach |
| Master Ability | You ignore half cover. Additionally, if you land an attack on a target more than 5ft away, it cannot move closer to you until the end of its next turn. |

#### Ravenbeak

This pike has a crescent blade on the side of the tip used to hook or slash. The added hook reduces the spear's penetration, but its utility makes up the difference. The master can redirect attacks and disarm with ease.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward, Heavy |
| Trained    | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Reach |
| Experience | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Heavy, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Master     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Entangle, Heavy, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Expert     | Two Handed, Melee, Brace, Disarm, Entangle, Heavy, Lunge, Reach, Trip |
| Master Ability | If an enemy misses you with a melee attack, you can cause it to target a creature of your choosing within its reach with that same attack roll. |

#### Trident

The war trident has sharpened, thicker tines and is used as an axe just as often as a spear. The master can trap, bind and disarm enemies with ease.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Thrown (20/60), Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Thrown (20/60), Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Disarm, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Deflect, Disarm, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Master Ability | You can deflect attacks against any target in reach. When you wield a trident with two hands, your enemy must succeed on a Reflex check or be disarmed when you deflect. |

\column

#### War Spear

A short, throw-balanced, banded spear with a hefty counterweight for one handed control or a two handed bludgeon. A master is a true war fighter, using spear techniques as ancient as the armies that employed them.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | Two Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Double Ended, Penetrate, Thrown (20/60), Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Double Ended, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Balanced, Double Ended, Penetrate, Puncture, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Master Ability | 	If you use this weapon one handed, you can use Double Ended as if you were using it with two. In two hands, you deal an additional d4 damage each time you hit with the main melee attack. |

#### Winged Spear

Small protrusions on either side of the spear head prevents a skewered target from closing on its wielder. A master keeps foes at bay while controlling their position.

| | |
|:-----------|:------|
| Untrained  | One Handed, Melee, Awkward |
| Trained    | One Handed, Melee, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Experience | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Master     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Nimble, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Expert     | One Handed, Melee, Disarm, Nimble, Thrown (30/120), Versatile |
| Master Ability | If you land an attack, you can move your target 5ft in a direction of your choice, and that target can't move closer to you until the end of its next turn. |

### Throwing Weapons

| Kunai | Piercing | d4 | d4 | d4 | d4 | d6 | 0.1 | 0.1 |
